		birth = yes
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
		effect = {
			agot_safe_set_location_history_effect = { CASTLE = title:k_braavos }
		}
	}
	8278.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			# add_trait = courtesan # AGOT TODO trait
			add_trait = refusing_marriage
		}

	}

		effect = {
			remove_nickname = yes
			# remove_trait = courtesan # AGOT TODO trait
			remove_trait = refusing_marriage
		}
	}
}
